for your child. That’s why we have developed Multiplication Dragons, to provide new, fun ways to engage with multiplication that stimulate ease of memorization and improved recall. We all know how difficult it is to remember things without using the proper tools, and Multiplication Dragons provides just that. Our brightly colored, unique, three-dimensional environments provide visual and auditory spaces in which children can learn by associating multiplication questions with a rhyme, an in-game location, and the dragon that asks the question.\r\n\r\nMultiplication Dragons helps increase memorization and ease of recall using two memory devices that reinforce each other: rhyme and the memory palace (a.k.a. the method of loci). It will introduce your child to the world of multiplication using 3D animated dragons that guide them through 12 different environments, including a lagoon, a Halloween inspired level, a mountain, caves, a winter setting, and more! Each of the 144 questions is asked by one of our many dragons, stationed in various locations and levels throughout the game. Questions are asked using a phrase that both rhymes with the answer, and relates to the particular surroundings of the level currently being played. Multiplication questions also appear onscreen and are read aloud, a design feature used to help young readers and those experiencing difficulty reading, and to provide our dragons with a bit of extra personality. \r\n\r\nWe draw on rhyme because it has been used in various ways and has stood the test of time as a mnemonic device. After all, how many times has the age-old “thirty days has September, April, June, and November” rhyme helped you to recall the number of days in a month? It has been used for generations, and proven its success over and over again. Our second memory device, the memory palace, is one of the oldest and most successful tools in the book! This method goes back to the ancient Greeks, and involves imagining a familiar environment (like your home) and associating the things to be remembered with particular areas or aspects of that environment.  The visual and spatial qualities of this form provide additional contact points that aid in the creation of cognitive associations with the thing that we want to remember. This creates more access routes for our brains to get at the desired information, and thus increases ease of recall. By using both of these methods together we have increased these possible cognitive associations even further, while providing you and your child with hours of fun!\r\n\r\nChildren will earn 1-3 stars based on the amount of correct answers given on a level, giving them the opportunity to return to a level and break their current score. They will also get an encouraging cheer from our dragons for each right or wrong answer, and unlock new levels by successfully completing a timetable level. They can also make use of an added visual cue by reviewing the timetable itself, and test recall by attempting quiz mode. Here, your child must answer questions without the rhymes, and in random order, simulating a school math test. El objetivo es lograr ese punto dulce donde las preguntas no son demasiado fáciles y no demasiado difíciles de lograr los máximos beneficios.\r\n \r\nMi motivación para desarrollar matemáticas amistosas creció de mirar a mis dos hijos interactuar con varias aplicaciones de matemáticas a través de los años. Mi preocupación con ésos era que los cabritos aprendieron presionar rápidamente los botones correctos sin mucha comprensión del tema.\r\n\r\nMatemáticas amigables se desarrolló para abordar algunas de estas preocupaciones. Con Matemáticas amigables, los niños no son cronometrados con el fin de permitirles tiempo para pensar, consolidar el conocimiento y entender verdaderamente los problemas. Las respuestas incorrectas no son penalizadas y la aplicación a menudo ofrece segundas oportunidades. Creo que este enfoque alienta el espíritu de aprendizaje y experimentación. El refuerzo positivo se utiliza, no la puntuación negativa. Esto evita que los niños formen actitudes negativas hacia las matemáticas y proteja su autoestima. El diseño visual simple de las aplicaciones ayuda a los niños a concentrarse en las matemáticas con un mínimo de distracciones, de modo que el aprendizaje puede transferirse fácilmente a las pruebas escolares y escenarios de la vida real.\r\n \r\nMatemáticas amigables proporciona a su hijo con recompensas en forma de logros coleccionables.
